# title:                Nyungwe do Novo Testamento<br>The New Testament in the Nyungwe Language of Mozambique

41001001	Kuyamba kwa Mafala Yabwino yakulewa bza Jezu Krixtu , Mwana wa Mulungu .
41001002	Ninga mpolofiti Isaya adanemba kuti : “ Mulungu adati , Ndin'dzatuma mtumiki wangu kutsogolo kwako , kuti akakondze njira yomwe iwe udzapitembo .
41001003	Fala la munthu wakukuwa mthengo ali kulewa kuti , ‘ Kondzani njira yakudzapitira Mbuya , thamulani miseu yomwe adzapitembo . ’ ”
41001004	N'cadidi adawoneka Juwau M'batizi kuthengo acilalika , “ Sandulikani mtima , mubatizidwe . Mulungu an'dzakulekererani bzakuipa bzanu . ”
41001005	Akhabwera kwa iye wanthu wakucokera kumbali zentse za Judeya na Jerusalemu . Iwo akhazimbula bzakuipa bzawo , Juwau akhawabatiza mumkulo wa Jorodau .
41001006	Iye akhabvala khanda la nchefu , akhamanga mciuno na mceka . Cakudya cace cikhali mabombo na uci bwa mthengo .
41001007	Akhalalika aciti : “ Pambuyo pangu pakubwera winango wamphambvu kuposa ine . Wakuti ine ndine wakusaya kufunika ngakhale kukotama kutsudzula thambo za xangu zace .
41001008	Ine ndakubatizani na madzi , tsono Iye an'dzakubatizani na Mzimu Wakucena . ”
41001009	Ntsiku zimwezo Jezu adabwera kucokera kuNazalee , mui ubodzi wa Galileya , acibatiziwa na Juwau mumkulo wa Jorodau .
41001010	Pakucoka mmadzimo , adawona kudzulu kwakufunguka , ndipo Mzimu Wakucena udabuluka kwa Iye ninga nkhangaiwa .
41001011	Kudzulu kudabveka mafala yakuti : “ Iwe ndiwe Mwana wangu wa pamtima . Nimbakomedwa nawe kwakukulu . ”
41001012	Nthawe imweyo Mzimu Wakucena udapitisa Jezu mthengo .
41001013	Adakhala kumweko ntsiku makumi manai . Sathani adamuyeza . Bzikhalipombo bzirombo bza mthengo . Tsono anjo zikhamutumikira .
41001014	Ataikhidwa kaidi Juwau , Jezu adayenda kuGalileya acilalika Mafala yabwino yakulewa bza Mulungu .
41001015	Adati : “ Nthawe yakwana . Bwafika Ufumu bwa Mulungu . Sandulikani mtima . Khulupirirani Mafala Yabwino . ”
41001016	Pakuyenda mmphephete mwa thawale la Galileya , Jezu adawona wanthu awiri , Sirimau na m'bale wace Andereya , akhatheya bwazi mmadzi , thangwe akhali akhongwe .
41001017	Adawauza Jezu : “ Imwe munditewere , ndikusanduseni akhongwe wa wanthu . ”
41001018	Adasiyeratu mabwaziyo ndipo adamutewera .
41001019	Atafamba pang'ono , adawona Tiyagu na Juwau , wana wa Zebedeu , omwe akhali mmwadiya kukondza mabwazi .
41001020	Jezu adawacemera , ndipo adasiya baba wawo Zebedeu mmwadiya pabodzi na anyabasa wace , acitewera .
41001021	Adayenda wentse kuKafernau . Yatafika ntsiku ya malinkhuma , Jezu adayenda mnyumba ya mapembero , acipfundzisa .
41001022	Wentse adadabwa na bzakupfundzisa bzace thangwe akhapfundzisa na utongi , akhasiyana ninga amisiri wa Mtemo .
41001023	Nthawe pang'ono adawoneka mnyumba ya mapemberomo munthu wakuphatidwa na mzimu wakuipa . Adalewa na kukuwa aciti :
41001024	“ Tina ciani na Imwe , Jezu wa Nazalee ? Kodi mwabwera kudzatidzonga ? Ndakudziwani kuti ndimwe Wakucena wa Mulungu . ”
41001025	Ndipo Jezu adalamulira mzimu wakuipayo , aciti , “ Khala zii , coka mwa munthuyu . ”
41001026	Pamwepo mzimu wakuipa ule udamutekenyesa munthuyo kwakukulu ucikuwa kwene-kwene , ndipo udacoka .
41001027	Wentse wale adadabwa kwakukulu acimbabvundzana , “ Kodi bzimwebzi n'ciani ? Cakupfundzisa cipsa cimweci ! Ambaitonga mizimu yakuipa na mphambvu , ndipo idamubvera . ”
41001028	Mwakamkulumize , mbiri yace idamwazika mbali zentse za Galileya .
41001029	Pambuyo pace Jezu adacoka kunyumba ya mapembero kule , adayenda kunyumba ya Sirimau na Andereya pabodzi na Tiyagu na Juwau .
41001030	Mibzala wa Sirimau akhadagona kwakufesuka , pamwepo wanthu adawuza Jezu bza matendayo .
41001031	Jezu adayenda aciwaphata boko aciwamusa , ndipo maferu yadamala . Na tenepo mai ule adawaphikira cakudya .
41001032	Maulo , latamira dzuwa , adawabweresa wentse wanthu kwa Jezu wakuduwala na wakuphatidwa na mizimu yakuipa .
41001033	Wentse wa mumzindamu adagwezekana pamsuwo .
41001034	Jezu adalimbisa azinji omwe akhabonera na matenda yakusiyana-siyana , acicosa mizimu yakuipa , aciiletsa kulewa-lewa thangwe idamuzindikira .
41001035	Macibese-bese kukhanati kucena , Jezu adamuka aciyenda kuthengo . Kumweko adakapembera .
41001036	Sirimau na andzace adamunyang'ana mbali zentse .
41001037	Atamugumana adamuuza kuti : “ Wanthu wentse ali kukunyang'anani . ”
41001038	Tsono Iye adatawira kuti : “ Mbatiyendeni tipite kumidzi inango pafupi na pam'pano , ndikalalike mafala kumweko . Thangwe ndibzo ndidabwerera . ”
41001039	Ndipo adayenda acilalika mnyumba zentse za mapembero kuGalileya kwentseko acicosa mizimu yakuipa .
41001040	Munthu winango wa mapere adabwera kwa Jezu . Adagodama acimudandaulira : “ Mucifuna , mungakwanise kundilimbisa . ”
41001041	Jezu adamubvera ntsisi . Adatambalisa boko lace acimukhuya acilewa , “ Cadidi , ndafuna , ulimbe ! ”
41001042	Panthawe ibodzi-bodziyo mapere yace yadamala , acicenesewa .
41001043	Ndipo Jezu adamuwuza kuti acoke acimucenjeza
41001044	kuti , “ Uleke kuwuza ali-yentse bzimwebzi , tsono uyende ukabziwonese kwa azibaba wantsembe , ukapereke ntsembe yomwe adalamula Mozeji ikakhale mboni kuti walimbadi . ”
41001045	Adandocoka pamwepo , munthuyo adayamba kumbazimbula bzentse na kumwaza nkhani . Na tenepo bzikhafunika lini kuti Jezu awoneke padeca mmizinda mwentse tsono akhakhala kuthengo . Ndipo wanthu akhambayenda kwa Iye kucokera mbuto na mbuto .
41002001	Patapita ntsiku pang'ono , Jezu adabwera pomwe kuKafernau . Bzidabveka kuti ali kunyumba .
41002002	Azinji adagumana mnyumbamo . Ndipo angakhale na pamsuwo pakhalibe mbuto yakupitira . Jezu , pakulewa mafala ya Mulungu .
41002003	Wanthu anai adanyamula bundukutu aciyenda naye .
41002004	Alibe kufika pafupi na Jezu thangwe ra mthithi wa wanthu . Adakwira pantsodzi ya nyumba , acinyasula ntsodziyo kulinganiza pakhana Jezu . Ndipo adamubulusa bundukutu ule pamacira .
41002005	Pakuwona cikhulupiriro cawo , Jezu adawuza bundukutuyo kuti , “ Mwana wangu , bzakuipa bzako bzalekereredwa . ”
41002006	Tsono pamwepo wakhadakhalambo amisiri wa Mtemo wa Mozeji . Iwo adayamba kubzibvundza mumtima mwawo kuti ,
41002007	“ Kodi Umweyu angalewe tani tenepo ? Kunyoza lini Mulungu kumweku ? Mbani angalekerere bzakuipa ? Ni Mulungu yekha ! ”
41002008	Ndipo Jezu mumzimu adadziwa kuti akhakumbuka bzimwebzi mumtima mwawo , na tenepo adawabvundza kuti , “ Thangwe ranyi mun'kumbuka bzimwebzi mmitima mwanu ?
41002009	Cakupusa n'ciponi , kumuwuza bundukutuyu kuti , ‘ Bzakuipa bzako bzalekereredwa , ’ ayai , ‘ Muka , tenga macira yako , uyende ? ’
41002010	Tsono kuti mudziwe Mwana-wa-Munthu ali nayo mphambvu pantsi pano yakulekerera bzakuipa , wonani . ” Ndipo adauza bundukutuyo ,
41002011	“ Iwe , muka , tenga macira yako , uyende kumui . ”
41002012	Pamaso pawentse , munthu ule adamuka , acitenga macira yace acicoka . Wanthu wentse adadabwa kwene-kwene , acipasa mbiri Mulungu acimbalewa , “ Cipo bzimwebzi tikanati kubziwona . ”
41002013	Jezu adayenda pomwe kugombe . Wanthu azinji adafika kumweko , ndipo Iye adawapfundzisa .
41002014	Pakufamba Jezu , adawona Levi , mwana wa Alifeu , akhadakhala pambuto ya basa la msonkho . Adamuuza aciti , “ Iwe , unditewere . ” Ndipo adamuka acimutewera .
41002015	Pomwe Jezu akhadya mnyumba mwa Levi , pakhana wanthu azinji wakupimisa msonkho na wanthu wakuphonya . Akhadya na Jezuyo pabodzi na wakupfundzira wace . Thangwe akhalipo azinji wa iwo omwe akhatewera iye .
41002016	Pakhali amisiri wa Mtemo wa Afaliseyu ndipo adawona kuti Jezu an'kudya na wanthu wakuphonya na wanthu wakupimisa msonkho , adabvundza wakupfundzira wace kuti , “ Thangwe ranyi an'kudya pabodzi na wakupimisa msonkho na wanthu wakuphonya ? ”
41002017	Jezu adabva bzimwebzo adawatawira kuti , “ Wanthu omwe mbakulimba an'nyangana lini mulapi . Wakuduwala ndiye an'nyangana mulapi ! Ine ndiribe kubwera kudzacemera wanthu wakulungama , tsono ndabwera kudzacemera wakuphonya . ”
41002018	Tsapano wakupfundzira wa Juwau M'batizi na Afaliseyu akhabzimana kudya . Wanthu adabwera kwa Jezu acimbabvundza aciti , “ Wakupfundzira wa Juwau na wakupfundzira wa Afaliseyu ambabzimana kudya . Thangwe ranyi wakupfundzira wanu ambabzimana lini ? ”
41002019	Jezu adatawira , “ Kodi andzace wa mwenekaciro msinda ya malowozi angasale kudya pomwe namwaliyo ali nawo ? Bzingacitike lini ! Iwo angasale lini kudya pomwe namwaliyo ali nawo .
41002020	Tsono in'dzafika nthawe yomwe an'dzawacosera namwaliyo . Nthawe imweyo an'dzabzimana kudya . ”
41002021	“ Palibe angasonere cakubvala ca kale na cigamba cipsa . Thangwe angacita tenepo , cigamba cire cimbanyothokera cicikuza mubo . Ndipo kung'ambika kwace kumbakhala kwakukulu kusiyana kale .
41002022	Ndipombo munthu angathire lini vinyu ipsa mmabudu ya khanda la kale . Thangwe angacita tenepo , mabudu yambang'ambika , ndipo vinyu ire imbataika . Mabuduyo nkhumala basa . Tsono bzin'funika kuikha vinyu mmabudu yapsa . ”
41002023	Pantsiku inango ya malinkhuma , Jezu akhapita mminda ya tirigu . Akhayenda tenepo , wakupfundzira wace adayamba kucosa ngala za tirigu acimbadya .
41002024	Pamwepo Afaliseyu adabvundza Jezu kuti , “ Thangwe ranyi wakupfundira wanu ali kucita bzomwe bzin'funika lini pantsiku ya malinkhuma ? ”
41002025	Iye adatawira , “ Thangwe ranyi mun'cita ninga mulibe kuwerenga bzomwe adacita David na andzace , pomwe wakhana njala ?
41002026	Iye adapita mnyumba ya Mulungu , panthawe yomwe Abiyatali akhali mkulu wa azibaba wa ntsembe , acikadya mkate wakuperekedwa kwa Mulungu ? Na tenepo mkate umweyo ukhali wakuletsedwa kuti winango ali-wentse adye , kupambula azibaba wa ntsembe wokha . Tsono adagawirambo andzace wale omwe akhali naye . ”
41002027	Ndipo Jezu pakupitiriza fala , adauza Afaliseyuwo kuti , “ Mulungu adaikha ntsiku ya malinkhuma kuti ikhale yakuthandiza wanthu . Alibe kulenga wanthu kuti akhale akapolo wa ntsiku ya malinkhuma .
41002028	Na tenepo Mwana-wa-Munthu ana mphambvu ngakhale kwa ntsiku ya malinkhuma . ”
41003001	Jezu adapita pomwe mnyumba yamapemphero . Momwemo mukhana munthu winango wakupunduka boko .
41003002	Wanthu winango akhanyangana thangwe ra kupasira mulandu Jezuyo , na tenepo akhanyang'anisa kuti aone angamulimbise munthuyo pa ntsiku ya kupuma .
41003003	Jezu adawuza munthu wakupundaka boko ule kuti , “ Ima , bwera kutsogolo kuno . ”
41003004	Ndipo adabvundza wanthu wale kuti , “ Kodi pa ntsiku ya malikhuma cin'bvumizidwa n'ciponi ? Kucita bzabwino , ayai kucita bzakuipa ? Kupulumusa moyo wa munthu , ayai kuudzonga ? ” Wanthuwo adakhala zii .
41003005	Jezu pakuo kuti wakhada wuma ndzelu mtima wace udamuwawa , pakuwona kuti akhali wanthu wamakani tenepo , ndipo adawayang'ana na ukali . Ndipo adamuwuza munthuyo kuti , “ Thamula boko lako . ” Iye adalithamula , ndipo boko lacero lidakhalambo bwino .
41003006	Pamwepo Afaliseyeu wale adacoka adakagumanizana na wanthu wa phati ra Herodi , kuti apangane njira yakuphera Jezu .
41003007	Jezu pabodzi na wakupfundzira wace adacoka pompale acienda kugombe la Galileya . Mthithi ukulu wa wanthu udamutewera .
41003008	Wanthu wale akhali wa ku Galileya , winango wa ku Judeya na ku Jerusalemu , winango wa ku Idumeya , na wang'ambo wa kumkulo wa Jorodau , ndipombo kucipande ca ku Tiru na Sidoni . Wentsenewo adafika kwa Iye , thangwe wakhabva bzizinji bzomwe Iye akhacita .
41003009	Jezu adauza wakupfundzira wace kuti amuikire mwadiya pafupi , akha gopesa kuti wanthu angayambe kum'psinyiza , thangwe ukhali mthithi ukulu
41003010	Na kuona kuti akhaciza wanthu azinji , ndipopo wentse omwe akhana matenda akhambagwinyana-gwinyana pakufuna kuti am'khuye .
41003011	Pomwe mizimu yakuipa ikamuwona ikhabzigwesa pantsi kutsogolo kwa Iye icimbakuwa kuti , “ Imwe ndimwe Mwana wa Mulungu . ”
41003012	tsono Iye akhambailetsa mwa mphambvu kuti ileke kumuzimbula .
41003013	Jezu adakwira ku phiri , ndipo adacemera wanthu omwe Iye akhawafuna , iwo adayenda komwe kukhana Iye .
41003014	Pamwepo adasankhula kumi na awiri , aciwacemera dzina la kuti , “ Atumiki . ” Adawauza kuti , “ Ndasakhula imwe kuti mumbakhale na ine , ndin'dzakutumani kukalalika ,
41003015	dicikupasani mphambvu yakuthotha mizimu yakuipa . ”
41003016	Wanthu kumi na awiri omwe adasankhuliwa mbawa : Sirimau ( omwe Jezu adamucemera Pedru ) ,
41003017	Tiyagu na m'bale wace Juwau , wana wa Zebedeu ( omwewo adawapasa dzina linango lakuti Aboanerje , bziri kulewa kuti “ Wakugopswa ninga Wana wa Ciphaliwali ” ) ,
41003018	Andereya , Filipe , Bartolomeyu , Mateyu , Tomasi , Tiyagu ( mwana wa Alifeu ) , Tadeyu , Sirimau ( wa phati landale la Azelote , )
41003019	ndipombo Judasi Iskaliote ( omwe adapereka Jezu . )
41003020	Pambuyo pace Jezu adaenda kunyumba , ndipo wanthu azinji adagumana pomwe , na tenepo Iye na wakupfundzira wace alibe kudzaone nthawe ya kuti adye .
41003021	Abale wace na kubva bzimwebzi , adabwera kuti adzamutenge , thangwe iwo akhati , “ Ali kucita nsala . ”
41003022	Amisiri winango wa Mtemo , omwe adabwera kucokera ku Jerusalemu , akhalewa kuti , “ Munthu omweyu waphatidwa na Belezebu . ” Akhalewa pomwe , “ Mphambvu zomwe umweyu ambacosera mizimu yakuipa nzakucokera kwa mkulu wa mizimuyo . ”
41003023	Na tenepo Jezu adacemera wanthu kuti abwere pafupi , aciwauza na mifanilizo kuti , “ Nandi Satana angabzithothe yekha ?
41003024	Wanthu wa mu umambo uli-wentse angayamba kusandukirana , umambo umwewo bunipitiriza lini .
41003025	Ndipo pomwe wanthu wa mbanja libodzi angayamba kugawika , banja limwero limpitiriza lini .
41003026	Na tenepo penu mu umambo wa Satana ngwakusandukirana na kupambulana , na tenepoyo bwamala .
41003027	“ palibe omwe angakwanise kupita mnyumba ya munthu wamphambvu acimubera bzinthu bzace akanati kum'manga . na tenepo ambatoma kum'manga acimubera bwino .
41003028	“ Ncadidi ndiri kulewa kuti wanthu angakwanise kulekereredwa bzakuipa bzentse , napo bzakulewa bzawo bzentse bzicikhala bzakunyoza Mulungu .
41003029	Tsono ali-yentse wakunyoza Mzimu Wakucena , an'dzalekereredwa lini bzakuipa bzace bzimbakhala bza kuyenda na kuyenda thagwe ni kaidi wa bzakuipa bzakusaya kumala . ”
41003030	Jezu adalewa bzimwebzi pakuwona kuti wanthu wale akhalewa kuti , “ Waphatidwa na mzimu wakuipa . ”
41003031	Mai na abale wace Jezu adabwera kumuiko . Adaima panja , adatuma wanthu kuti akamucemere .
41003032	Wanthu azinji akhadakhala acimuzungulira . Ndipo wale adamuuza kuti , “ Mai wako na abale wako ali panjapa , ali kukucemera . ”
41003033	Tsono Iye adati , “ Mai wangu ! Abale wangu ! Waponi pomwe ? ”
41003034	Pamwepo adayang'ana wanthu wale omwe akhadakhala acimuzungulira aciti , “ Ine mai wangu na abale wangu mbawa .
41003035	Ali-yentse omwe ancita bzomwe Mulungu an'funa , womwewo ndiwo am'bale wangu , na mai wangu . ”
41004001	Jezu adayamba pomwe kupfundzisa mphephete mwa thawale la Galileya . Wanthu azinji adakatsokhana naye , na tenepo Iye adapakira mmwadiya , Wanthu wentse akhali kunja mphepete mwa thawalero ,
41004002	ndipo Jezu akhamba wapfundzisa bzizinji mmifananizo . Pakuwapfundzisa adati ,
41004003	“ Tetekerani ! Munthu winango adaenda ku kabzala ,
41004004	Pakubzala mbeu ire inango idagwera munjira , ndipo mbalame zidabwera ziciidya .
41004005	inango idagwera pa ntsongolobwe , pomwe pakhalibe mataka mazinji . Idamera kankulumize , thangwe matakayo yakhalibe kufika pantsi .
41004006	pomwe dzuwa lidakwira , idapsa iciuma , thangwe ikhalibe mizi
41004007	inango idagwera pa minga , pakukula minga ire idapsinyiza mbeu , na tenepo iyo iribe kudzabereka
41004008	Ndipo mbeu inango idagwera pa mataka yabwino . Idamera bwino icikula , ndipo icibereka . inango ikhana bzisapo makumi matatu , inango makumi matanthatu , inango dzana . ”
41004009	Ndipo Jezu adati , “ Ule ana makutu yakubva , abve ! ”
41004010	Pomwe Jezu akhali payekha , wakupfundzira khumi na awiri wale pabodzi na anango omwe akhali pabodzi naye adamubvundza bza mifananizo ire
41004011	Iye adawatawira kuti , “ Imwepo Mulungu adakuzimbulirani cintsintsi ca Umambo wace . Tsono anangowo omwe ali kunja , bzentse ambandobzibvera mmifananizo yokha ,
41004012	kuti ‘ Kuyang'ana ayang'ane , tsono acisaya kuwona cinthu , ndipo kubva abve cadidi , tsono acisaya kubva cinthu , kuti angasandulike mtima , ndipo Mulungu angadzawalekerere . ’ ”
41004013	Pambuyo pace Jezu adawabvundza kuti , “ Penu imwe muli kubvesesa lini mfananizo uyu , mungabvesese tani mifananizo inango ?
41004014	Wakubzala mbeu ule ni omwe ambabzala mafala ya Mulungu .
41004015	Mbeu zakugwera munjira zire bziri kulewa wanthu omwe ambabva mafala ya Mulungu . Tsono nthawe yomweyo Satana ambabwera , acicosa mafala yale .
41004016	Mbeu zakubzalidwa pa ntsongolobwe zire bziri kulewa wanthu omwe ambabva mafala ya Mulungu , nthawe yomweyo acitambira na mpfatso .
41004017	Tsono thangwe kuti mafalayo yalibe mizi , wanthuwo ambakhala nthawe ing'ono-ng'ono yokha . ingandofika mphica ayai matsautso thangwe ra mafala yale , nthawe yomweyo wanthuwo ambabwerera mmbuyo .
41004018	Mbeu zakubzalidwa pa minga zire bziri kulewa wanthu omwe ambabva mafala ya Mulungu .
41004019	Tsono kufuna-funa bza pantsi-pano , kufunisisa nthaka na kusirira bzinthu bzinango bzizinji bzimbapitambo nkhusayisa mphambvu mafala yale , na tenepo yambadzabereka lini bzisapo .
41004020	ndipo mbeu zakubzalidwa pa mataka yabwino bziri kulewa wanthu omwe wambabva mafala ya Mulungu , waciyatambira . wacibereka bzisapo , yinango makumi matatu , yinango makumi matanthatu , yinango dzana . ”
41004021	Tsono Jezu adawabvundza kuti , “ Kodi wanthu ambatenga lampalina acigwanankira na mtsuko , ayai kuibisa mfunfuntsi mwa talimba ? Ambaikha lini padeca ?
41004022	Na tenepo ciri-centse cakubisika cin'dzaoneka , pomwe ciri-centse ca kabise-bise bzin'dzazimbuka padeca .
41004023	Ule ana makutu yakubva , abve ! ”
41004024	Adawauza pomwe kuti , “ Mumbakhale na tcero na mafala yomwe mumbabva . [ maphatidwe uncita winango ] Mulungu an'dzaphatisambo basa cibodzibodzico pakuweruzambo imwepo , na tenepo kwa imwepo an'dzathimizira .
41004025	Pamwepo omwe ana cinthu kale , an'dzamuthimizira cinango . Tsono omwe alibe cinthu , cing'ono comwe anaco an'dzamutengera basi . ”
41004026	Jezu adalewa pomwe kuti , Umambo bwa Mulungu tingandendemeze na munthu wakubzala mbeu mmunda .
41004027	Omwe ambandogona usiku na masikati , nthawe yentseneyo mbeu yomwe adabzala ire idamera icikula , mwenekaciroyo ne kudziwa momwe bziri kucitikira .
41004028	Pamwepo mataka yambaberekesa pomwe mbeu ire yokha-yokha . ambayamba ni nyakamera , zicibwera ngala-ngala , pambuyo pace bzisapo mungala-ngala mule bzimbakhuma .

42006017	Ndipo iye adapolika nawo kucigwa komwe kukhana ateweri wace azinji kwene-kwene . Ndipo nthithi wa wanthumbo azinji akhadacokera kuJudeya na kuJeruzalema na kumphete kwa madzi ya nyandza ya Tiru na Sidonya .

42006019	Ndipo wanthu wentse akhafuna kumukhuya , thangwe iye akhana mphambvu . Na tenepo adawalimbisa wentse .
42006020	Ndipo iye adanyang'anisa ateweri wace , aciti : Wakusimbidwa ndimwe wakusauka , thangwe Umambo bwa Mulungu mbwanu .
42006021	Wakusimbidwa ndimwe omwe muna njala tsapano-lino , thangwe mundzakhuta . Wakusimbidwa ndimwe omwe lero muli kulira nakuti mundzaseka .

42006023	na tenepo dzakondweni ntsiku imweyo , mucidzasekera , thangwe mabaibai yanu kudzulu yan'dzakhala makulu kwene-kwene . Nakuti azibabawo adacitambo bzimwebzi kuna apolofeta .

42006033	Penu imwepo mumbacita bzinthu bzabwino kuna wale omwe ambakucitiranimbo bzabwino okha , kodi mun'dzatambira mabaibai yanyi ? Nakuti anyakuphonya ambacitambo bzibodzi-bodzibzo .

42006036	Khalani na ntsisi ninga Babanu ngwa ntsisimbo .
42006037	Lekani kumbatonga andzanu kuti Mulungu adzasaye kukutonganimbo . Lekani kumanga mulandu andzanu kuti Mulungu adzasaye kukumanganimbo . Khululukirani mitima andzanu kuti Mulungu adzakukhululukirenimbo .

42006041	Kodi thangwe ranyi uli kukwanisa kuwona manthongo yomwe yali m'maso mwa mwanzako , ucisaya kubva citsetswa comwe ciri m'maso mwako ?
42006042	Ungauze tani mwandzako kuti : “ Bwera ndikupukuse manthongo . Kodi iwepo uli kubva lini citsetswa comwe ciri m'maso mwakomo ? Mpfaka-faka ! Toma kucosa citsetswa comwe ciri m'maso mwakomu kuti undzawone bwino yali m'maso mwa mwandzakomu .

42008039	“ Bwerera ! Ndoko kumui ukafotokozere andzako bzentse bzomwe Mulungu wakucitirabzi . Na tenepo iye adayenda mu mzinda acikafotokoza bzentse bzomwe bzidacitikabzo .

42010028	Na tenepo Jezu adamuwuza kuti : “ Watawira bwino . Cita bzimwebzo na tenepo un'dzakhala na moyo wa kusaya kumala . ”

42010031	Tsono baba wa ntsembe mwinango akhandobzipitirambo na njira , pomwe adamuwona , ndipo iye adamutsembera .

42010041	Ndipo Mbuya adamutawira aciti : ' ' Marta , Marta ! Una ciberefuwa nakucita bzinthu bzizinji .
42010042	Tsono , cinthu cibodzi cin'funika . Na tenepo Maliya wasankhula cinthu cabwino . Ndipo palibe munthu omwe angadzamutengere . ”
42011001	Pantsiku inango Jezu akhapemba pambuto ibodzi . Pomwe adamala kupembako , mteweri wace m'bodzi adamuwuza kuti : “ Mbuya , tipfundzisenimbo kupemba , ninga momwe Juwau akhapfundzisira ateweri wace . ”
42011002	Ndipo iye adawauza kuti : Mukapemba mbalewani kuti : Baba , dzina lanu likhale na mbiri . Umambo bwanu mbabubwere .
42011003	Tipaseni cakudya cathu ca ntsiku zentse .
42011004	Mutirekere bzakuipa bzathu , ninga ifembo tinilekera wale omwe ambatiphonyera Ndipo lekani kutilekerera kuti tipumpsidwe .
42011005	Ndipo Jezu adawawuza kuti : Mbani wa imwepo omwe acikhala na xamwali wace acidzamugugudzira pakati pausiku acimuuza kuti : ndikumbizembo magapa matatu ya ufa .
42011006	Nakuti ndabweredwa na mulendo . Na tenepo ndiribe cakumupasa .
42011007	Ndipo xamwali waceyo acimutawira ali m'nyumba kuti : “ Leka kundinesa ! Nakuti ine ndafunga kale msuwo . Nakuti ine na wana wangu tagona kale . Na tenepo ine-pano ningamuke lini kuti ndidzakupase cinthu . ”
42011008	Tsono dziwani kuti napo akasaya kumuka kuti amupase nakuti ni xamwali wace . Ndipo iye an'zalamuka basi thangwe la kumunesa na kumubwerera nthawe imweire . Ndipo iye an'dzamupasa bzentse bzomwe iye an'funa .
42011009	Na tenepo ndinikuwuzani kuti kumbirani , ndipo mun'dzapasidwa . Lingani , ndipo mun'dzabziwona . Gugudzani , ndipo mun'dzakufunguliridwa .
42011010	Nakuti munthu wentse omwe an'kumbira ambapasidwa . Na ule omwe ambalinga ambabziwona . Na ulembo omwe ambagugudza ambafunguliridwa .
42011011	Kodi mbani baba-munthu pakati panupa penu mwanace wakumbira ntsomba angamupase nyoka ?
42011012	Ayai penu iye wakumbira dzai angamupase nyankalize ?
42011013	Imwepo ndimwe wanthu wakuipa , tsono mumbadziwa kupasa bzinthu bzabwino wana wanu . Ndipo Babanu wa kudzulu ambapereka bzinthu bzabwino kuposa imwepo . Na tenepo an'dzapasa Mzimu wa Kucena kuna wale omwe an'dzamukumbira !
42011014	Pantsiku ibodzi Jezu akhazula ciwanda comwe cikhadasandusa munthu ubewewe . Pomwe ico cidacoka , munthuyo adayamba adalewa-lewa . Na tenepo wanthu azinji adasusumwa .
42011015	Tsono wanthu winango akhambalewa kuti : “ Omweyu ali kuzula bziwanda mudzina la Berezebu , mkulu wa bziwanda . ”
42011016	Na tenepo wanthu winango akhafuna kuyezera Jezu , ndipo adamukumbira kuti awalatize cizindikiro ca kudzulu .
42011017	Tsono Jezu akhadziwa kale ndzeru zawo , ndipo iye adawawuza kuti : Dzindza libodzi la wanthu likapambulana iro lin'pfudzika . Na tenepo banja libodzi likabzigawa ndipo iro lin'pasuka .
42011018	Penu wa kwa Sathanimbo adabzigawa , ndipo ufumu bwacebo bungayenderere lini ! Nakuti muli kulewa kuti ine-pano ndiri kuzula bziwanda mu dzina la Berezebu .
42011019	Penu ine-pano ndiri kuzula bziwanda mudzina la Berezebu , kodi wana wanuambo ali kuzula mudzina la yani ? Penu n'bzimwebzo , iwo ndiwo an'dzakuyeruzani .
42011020	Tsono , penu ine-pano ndiri kuzula bziwanda na mphambvu za Mulungu , umambo bwacebo bwakufikirani cadidi .
42011021	Penu munthu nyamphambvu akatenepo ali kulindira pamui pace . Ndipo bzinthu bzacebzo bzimbakhocherereka bwino .
42011022	Tsono pakawonekambo munthu mwinango nyamphambvu kuposa iye , akamenyana naye acimukunda ambamutolera bzifuzo bzomwe akhathembanabzobzo . Ndipo acigawira wanthu bzinthu bzacebzo .
42011023	Na tenepo munthu omwe ngwangu lini ni muwengi wangu . Na ule omwe an'dithandiza lini kukonkhobza iye animwaza .
42011024	Ndipo ciwanda cikacoka mu munthu , ico cimbayenda mu mbuto zakusaya madzi kuti cikapume . Ndipo cikasaya mbuto , cimbalewa kuti : “ Tsapano ndini bwerera kumui kwangu komwe ndacokera . ”
42011025	Ndipo ico cikafika , cimbadzawona nyumbayo idapsairidwa ndipo idacena .
42011026	Na tenepo ico cimbayenda kukatenga pomwe bzinango bzinomwe bzakuipa kuposa ico , bzicikhala m'mwemo . Ndipo unthu bwace mumbadzalemwa kuipa kuposa pakuyamba .
42011027	Pomwe akhalewa bzimwebzopo , mkazi m'bodzi adakuwa pakati panthithi wa wanthu aciti : “ Wakusimbidwa ni mamako omwe adakubala na kukumamisa ! ”
42011028	Tsono iye adatawira aciti : Ne-ne-ne , wakusimbidwe mbale omwe ambabva fala la Mulungu aciliteweza . ”
42011029	Pomwe wanthu azinji akhakonchezana , Jezu adalewa kuti : “ Dzindza la wanthu wakuipa ! Iwo an'funa cizindikiro . Tsono palibe cizindikiro cinango comwe cin'citike kuposa comwe cidacitikira Jona .
42011030	Nakuti Jona akhali cizindikiro kuna wanthu wa kuNiniva . Na tenepo Mwana wa Munthu ni cizindikirombo kuna dzindza limweri .
42011031	Ndipo Mambokazi wa Kunyantsi an'dzalamuka pantsiku yakutongedwa pakati pawanthu , ndipo acimanga mulandu ntundu omweyo wa wanthu . Nakuti mambokaziyo adacokera kwa kuyambira dziko kuti akabve ndzeru za Salomau . Tsono ali panoyu ni mkulu kuposa Salomauyo .
42011032	Na tenepo wanthu wa kuNiniva an'dzamukambo pantsiku ya kutongedwa dzindza limwero kuti adzalimangembo mulando . Nakuti iwo adakhumbula bzakuipa bzawo pomwe Jona adapaliza . Tsono ali panoyu ni mkulu kuposa Jonayo .
42011033	Ndipo palibe munthu ambaphatiza m'bvuniko aciubisa ayai aciukha m'mpfumpfuntsi mwa bwalizo . Tsono iye ambauikha padzulu , kuti wanthu omwe an'pitawo awone ceza .
42011034	Na tenepo maso yako ndico ceza ca thupi lako . Penu iyo yali bwino na thupi lakombo lina ceza . Tsono penu yali lini bwino na thupi lakombo lina m'dima .
42011035	Ndipo , cenjerani kuti ceza ciri m'maso mwanuco cileke kukhala mdima .
42011036	Na tenepo penu thupi lako lentse liribe m'mdima na pang'onopo , ndipo lin'dzayetima ninga momwe umbatoyera mbvuniko ukaugasa .
42011037	Pomwe Jezu adamala akhalewalewa , m'falizeu m'bodzi adamucemera kuti akadye naye . Na tenepo iye adayenda acikakhala patsantsali la kudyera .
42011038	Tsono m'falizeuyo adadabwa pomwe adamuwona kuyamba kudya acisaya kusamba m'manja .
42011039	Ndipo Mbuya adamuwuza kuti : “ Afalizeumwe mumbatsuka kunja kokha mikombo na ndiro . Tsono mitima yanu nja ndewo na mingululi .
42011040	Mapsirumwe ! Kodi ule omwe adakondza kunja , ni m'bodzo-bodzi lini omwe adakondza mkati ?
42011041	Tsono tomani kuthandiza anyakusauka na bzinthu bzomwe munabzo . Na tenepo bzinthu bzentsenebzo bzin'dzacena .
42011042	Tsoka kuna imwe afalizeu ! Nakuti imwepo mumbateweza mitemo yentse ya Mozeji , mumbapereka kuna Mulungu cacikhumi ca mbeu zentse za m'munda . Tsono mumbayebwa cilungamo na lufoi la Mulungu . Na tenepo citani bzimwebzi mucisaya kuyebwa bzinangobzi .
42011043	Tsoka kuna imwe afalizeu ! Nakuti imwepo mumbafuna kukhala m'mipando ya ulemu ya m'nyumba zakupembera na kumbamusidwa m'misika .
42011044	Tsoka kuna imwe afalizeu ! Nakuti kuteweza mitemo yanu bzidandendemera ninga munthu ali kupita nthenje aciponda nthutu nakusaya kudziwa , uko ni mukho . ”
42011045	Ndipo m'pfundzisi wa ntemo m'bodzi adamuwza kuti : “ Misiri , mafala yamweya muli kutukwana nayo ife-panombo . ”
42011046	Tsono Jezu adamutawira aciti : “ Tsokambo kuna imwepo apfundisi wa ntemomwe . Nakuti mumbanyamuza andzanu mitolo yakulemera kwene-kwene . Tsono imwepo mumbawathandiza lini kuwasendza napo na cala cokha .
42011047	Tsoka pomwe kuna imwepo thangwe mumbakondza nthutu za apolofetapolofeta omwe adaphedewa na azibabanu .
42011048	Na tenepo imwepo ndimwe mboni thangwe mwatawira bzinthu bzomwe adacita azibabanu . Nakuti iwo adapha apolofetawo ndipo imwepo muli kuwakondzera nthutu .
42011049	Na tenepo , Mulungu udziwi bwace adalewa kuti : ' Ine ndin'dzatumiza apolofeta na atumiki , tsono winango an'dzaphedwa na winango an'dzathothedwa .
42011050	Na tenepo ntundu omweyu un'dzamangidwa mulandu na thangwe ra kupha apolafetawo , kuyambira pakulengedwa kwa dziko .
42011051	Ndipo kutomera pakuphedwa kwa Aberi mpaka kwa Zakaliya , iwo omwe adaphedwera pakati pamphatso na mbuto yakucena . Ndikukuuzani cadidi kuti ntundu omweyu un'dzamangidwa mulandu .
42011052	Tsoka pomwe kuna imwe apfundzisi wa ntemo ! Nakuti mwatenga mpfunguliso wa ndzeru . Na tenepo imwepo mulibe kupita m'mwemo muciphingizambo pomwe andzanu omwe akhafuna kupita . ”
42011053	Pomwe iye adacoka pamwepo , apfundzisi wa ntemo na afalizeu adamuwenga kwene-kwene . Ndipo iwo akhamupikixa na mibvundzo .
42011054	Na tenepo iwo akhanyang'ana mathangwe kuti iye angawatawira amumange nayo mulandu .
42012001	Panthawe imweyo bzulu na bzulu bza wanthu adakhonchezana ndipo iwo akhapsindizana . Na tenepo Jezu adatoma kulewa-lewa na ateweri wace aciti : Cenjerani na mapfundziso ya afalizeu , nakuti ngakunama .
42012002	Ndipo palibe cinthu cakumpsinkhika comwe cin'dzasaya kukundulidwa , na cire comwe cin'dziwika lini ndipo cin'dzadziwika .
42012003	Na tenepo bzentse bzomwe mudalewa pam'dima bzin'dzabzeka pakungwerewera . Na bzentsembo bzomwe mwalewa na kawere-were m'gwangwa , bzin'dzakuwidwira pantsodzi .
42012004	Jezu adawawuza pomwe kuti : Axamwali wangu ! Ndiri kukuwuzani kuti muleke kugopa wanthu omwe ambapha thupi lokha , akamala bzimwebzo palibe cinango comwe ambacita .
42012005	Tsono ine-pano ndin'funa kukulatizani omwe an'funika kugopedwa . Ndipo gopani ule omwe akapha munthu , ana mphambvu ya kumuthusa m'cidindi ca moto . N'cadidi kuti omweyo m'mugopeni .
42012006	Kodi munthu ambagulisa lini ajolo axanu na konto ziwiri basi ? Na tenepo palibe na m'bodzi yekha omwe Mulungu ambamuyebwa .
42012007	Napo tsisi lentse la mumsolo mwanuli , Mulungu adaliwerenga kale . Lekani kugopa , thangwe imwepo mun'funika kwene-kwene kuposa ajolowo .
42012008	Ndipo Jezu adalewa pomwe kuti : Ule omwe an'dibvuma pakati pawanthu , na Mwana wa Munthu an'dzamubvumambo pakati paanjo wa Mulungu .
42012009	Tsono ule omwe an'dilamba pakati pawanthu , ndipo Mwana wa Munthu an'dzamulambambo pakati paanjo wa Mulungu .
42012010	Ule omwe an'tukwana Mwana wa Munthu , Mulungu an'dzamulekera bza kuipa bzace . Tsono ule omwe an'nyoza Mzimu Wakucena , Mulungu an'dzamulekera lini .
42012011	Ndipo akadzakutengani acidzayenda namwe kunyumba zakupembera , ayai kuna atongi na kumphambvu za umangi , dzalekeni kukhala na thupo kuti mun'dzatawira ciani ayai mun'dzalewa ciani .
42012012	Nakuti Mzimu Wakucena un'dzakupfundzisani panthawe imweyo kuti mun'dzalewa ciani .
42012013	Munthu mwinango pantithipo adakuwa kuti : “ Misiri , uzani m'bale wanguyu kuti tigawane utaka bwa babathu . ”
42012014	Ndipo Jezu adamutawira kuti : “ Nandi iwe ! Kodi mbani adandipasa basa la kutonga na kugawira wanthu utaka ? ”
42012015	Ndipo iye adawawuza pomwe kuti : Khalani na cheru kuti muleke kucita m'tima loko-loko na cinthu , nakuti moyo wa munthu ulibe basa na kuwanda kwa bzinthu bzacebzo .
42012016	Na tenepo iye adawatsikira pomwe matere aciti : “ Pakhana munda wa munthu m'bodzi nyakudala omwe udakosa bzakudya bzizinji kwene-kwene .
42012017	Ndipo iye adakumbuka mumtima mwace kuti : ' kodi ine-pano phoso limweri ndini likoya kuponi ?
42012018	Ndipo iye adalewa kuti : ' Ndin'dzapfudza magwangwa yanguya ndicidzamanga yanango makulu ndipo ndicidzakoya m'mwemo phosolo na bzinthu bzangu bzinango .
42012019	Pamwepo ine ndin'dzalewa na mumtima kuti : ' Moyo wangu una bzinthu bzentse bzomwe un'funa bza magole mazinji , tsapano derekha , udye , umwe , udakondwa . '
42012020	Tsono Mulungu adamuwuza kuti : ' Nandi dzengawe ! Usiku buno unifa iwepo . Kodi apa mbani an'sala na bzinthu bzomwe udakoyabzi ? '
42012021	Na tenepo , bzidakhala ninga munthu nyamingululi omwe ana cuma cizinji kwene-kwene , tsono alibe kupasa Mulungu cinthu .
42012022	Na tenepo Jezu adawacenjeza ateweri wace kuti : “ Lekani kukhala na thupo mumtima kuti mun'dzadyanyi ayai kuti mun'dzabvalanyi nthupi mwanumu .
42012023	Nakuti moyo ngukulu kuposa cakudya , na thupimbo lina basa kuposa cakubvala .
42012024	Ndipo onani akhungubwe . Iwo ambalima lini , ambabvuna lini , alibe magota ayai magwangwa . Ndipoi Mulungu ambawadyesa basi . Tsono imwepo mun'funika kwene-kwene kuposa mbalamezo !
42012025	Kodi mbani angakhale nathupo na moyo wace ndipo angakwanise kubzithumizira pomwe ntsiku ibobzi ?
42012026	Na tenepo penu imwe mun'kwanisa lini kucita bzinthu kang'onobzi , thangwe ranyi muna thupo na bzinthu bzinango ?
42012027	Tsono onani maluwa momwe yambakulira ! Ndipo iyo yambaphata lini basa ayai kusona bzakubvala . Napo Salomau na mbiri yentse yomwe akhanayo , akhalibe bzakubvala bzakugaka bwino kuposa maluwayo .
42012028	Ninga momwe Mulungu ambabvazikira mausuwa ya mthengo , yomwe yambamera ninga lero mangwana yacipsa na moto . Napo imwepombo ndimwe wanthu wakusaya cikhulupiropa , kodi iye angakwanise lini kukubvazikanimbo ?
42012029	Na tenepo lekani kukhala na thupo kuti mun'dzadyanyi ayai kuti kun'dzamwanyi .
42012030	Thangwe wanthu wa mudziko , ndiwo ambafunisisa bzentsenebzi . Tsono Babanu an'dziwa kale kuti imwepo mun'bzifuna .
42012031	Tomani mwanyang'ana umambo bwa Mulungu . Ndipo bzinthu bzinangobzo Iye an'dzakupasani .
42012032	Nandi tubzifuwo tuwangu , lekani mantha ! Nakuti Babanu an'funa kukupasani umambo bwace .
42012033	Na tenepo gulisani bzinthu bzanu , mupase anyakusauka . Ndipo sonani mabudu yomwe yan'sakala lini . Nakuti cuma ca kudzulu cimbamala lini , komweko kulibe mbava , ayai manthedza kuti yangajete .
42012034	Nakuti pale pomwe pana cuma canu na mtima wanu uli pamwepombo .
42012035	Ndipo kondzekerani kuti muphate basa . Mibvuniko yanu ikhali idagaka .
42012036	Na tenepo khalani ninga anyabasa ali kudikhira mbuya , omwe an'bwerera kucokera kucikondweso ca malowozi . Ndipo iye akafika akadzagugudza msuwo mudzam'fungulire na kankulumize .
42012037	Ndipo wakusimbidwa mbaanyabasa wale omwe Mbuya akabwera an'dzawagumana adamudikhira . Ndiri kukuwuzani cadidi kuti iye an'dzawakhazika patsantsali la kudyera iye acibvala ndipo aciwatumikira .
42012038	Ndipo wakusimbidwa pomwe n'bale omwe mbuya an'dzawagumana adamukhalilira napo n'pakati pausiku ayai madandakweca .
42012039	Na tenepo dziwani kuti penu mwenekaciro nyumba angadadziwa nthawe yakubwera mbava , ndipo iye angadailekerera lini kuti ichole nyumbayo .
42012040	Na tenepo khalani wakukondzekera nakuti Mwana wa Munthu an'dzabwera panthawe yomwe imwe mukhadikhira lini .
42012041	Pamwepo Pedru adabvunza kuti : “ Nandi Mbuya , kodi muli kutsikira matereya ife tekha ayai kuna wanthu wentse ? ”
42012042	Ndipo Mbuya adatawira aciti : “ Kodi mbani msunga cuma wandzeru na wakukhulupirika , omwe mbuya angadzamusiire panyumba pace kuti ambadzagawire phoso andzace nthawe ikakwana ?
42012043	Wakusimbidwa ni msunga cuma ule omwe mbuya wace akabwera an'dzam'gumana acicita tenepo .
42012044	N'cadidi kuti iye an'dzam'pasa mpando ukulu wakumbawonerera bzinthu bzace bzentse .
42012045	Tsono nyabasa ule omwe angadakumbuka kuti : “ mbuya wangu ali kucedwa kubwera . ” Ndipo iye aciyamba kutukwana na kumenya anyabasa andzace wale , wacimuna na wacikazi . Ndipo acimbadya na kumwa aciledzera . ”
42012046	Ndipo pantsiku yomwe an'dzafika mbuya waceyo pomwe angadzafika mbuya waceyo , pantsiku yomwe iye akhamudikhira lini . Ndipo iye adzamulum , acimucosa basa .
42012047	Napo iye acidziwisisa bzomwe bzin'funa mbuya wace iye akasaya kucita na kubziteweza , adzachangidwa kwene-kwene .
42012048	Ndipo ule omwe akhandziwa lini bzomwe bzikhafuna mbuya wace , akacita bzinthu bzakuipa , na tenepo an'dzachangidwa pang'ono . Tsono ule omwe an'tambira bzizinji an'dzasundidwambo bzizinji . Na ulembo ule omwe an'khulupiridwa na bzinthu bzizinji , iye an'dzasundidwambo bzizinji .
42012049	Ndipo ine ndidabwerera kudzaphatiza moto padziko la pantsi . Na tenepo ndikhafuna kuti nthawe ino ukhale uli kugaka kale !
42012050	Ine-pano ndina batizo linango kuti nditambire . Tsono ndina ciya mpaka iro licitike .
42012051	Kodi mun'kumbuka kuti ndidabweresa m'tendere pantsi pano ? Ne-ne-ne , ndidabweresa kupambulana .
42012052	Na tenepo kucokera lero mpaka kutsogolo , banja la wanthu axanu lin'dzapambulana . Wanthu atatu an'dzawengana na wanthu awiri . Ndipo awiri acidzawenganambo na atatuwo .
42012053	Ndipo baba-munthu an'dzawengana na mwana . Ndipo mwana aciwenganambo na baba munthuyo . Na ma-munthu a'ndzawenagana na mwanace wacikazi . Ndipo mwana wacikaziyo acidzawenganambo na mamaceyo . Mibzala an'dzawengana na mulowola . Na mulowolayo acidzawenganambo na mibzalayo .
42012054	Ndipo Jezu adawawuza pomwe wanthu wale kuti : “ Mukawona m'tambo uli kukwira ucicokera kumadokero mumbalewa kuti mbvula in'bvumba . Ndipo iyo imbabvumba cadidi .
42012055	Ndipo mukabva condzi cicicokera kunyantsi , mumbalewa kuti lero kunipsa . Na tenepo kumbapsa cadidi .
42012056	Mpfakafaka ! Imwepo mumbadziwa kufotokoza makhalidwe ya pantsi na kudzulu . Kodi thangwe ranyi mun'saya kudziwa kuthumbudzula bzinthu bzomwe bziri kucitika nyengo inobzi ?
42012057	Kodi thangwe ranyi mumbasaya kutongana mwekha bzabwino ?
42012058	Penu una mulandu na munthu , iye akafuna kukakutongesa kumphala , toma wayezera kuyanjana naiye munjira , kuti asaye kukakulewera kuna m'tongi . Ndipo m'tongiyo aleke kukupereka kumphambvu ya umangi . Kuti iye asayembo kukakufungira m'kawoko .
42012059	Na tenepo diri kukuwuza kuti un'dzacoka lini m'kawokomo penu ukanati kumala kulipira mulanduyo .
42013001	Panthawe imweyo pakhana wanthu omwe adawuza Jezu nkhani ya agalileu omwe adaphedwa ndipo Pilato adasanganiza mulopa na ntsembe zawo .
42013002	Na tenepo iye adawabvundza kuti : “ Kodi mun'kumbuka kuti agalileu omwe adaphedwa akhali anyakuphonya kwene-kwene kuposa andzawo , kuti abonere tenepoyo ?
42013003	Ndiri kukuwuzani kuti , akhali lini . Tsono mukasaya kukhumbula mun'mala mwentse ninga iwombo .
42013004	Ayai kodi mun'kumbuka kuti wanthu khumi na asere omwe adagweredwa na cinyumba ca Silowee ciciwapha , akhali anyakuphonya kwene-kwene kuposa wanthu wentse wa kuJeruzalema ?
42013005	Ndiri kukuwuzani pomwe kuti akhali lini . Tsono imwepo mukasaya kukhumbula mun'mala mwentse ninga iwombo .
42013006	Ndipo Jezu adawatsikira matere aciti : “ Munthu m'bodzi akhadabzala mkuyu m'munda mwace . Ndipo adayenda kuti akache nkhuyu , tsono iye adazisaya .
42013007	Na tenepo iye adawuza nyakulindira mundayo kuti : ' Kwapita magole matatu pomwe ndidaubzala mkuyuyu . Lero ndanyang'ana-nyang'ana mwentsenemu tsono ndiribe kuwona cinthu . Ugwate ! Thangwe ranyi uli kundodya mbuto pamwepa ? '
42013008	Tsono iye adatawira kuti : ' Ulekeni , Mbuya , gole lino lokha . Ine-pano nin'ucerera-cerera ndicikha manyowa . '
42013009	Penu un'dzabala , n'psabzabwino basi . Ayai ukadzasaya kubala ndipo mudzaugwate bwino . ”
42013010	Pasabudu linango Jezu akhapfundzisa m'nyumba ya kupembera ibodzi .
42013011	Ndipo m'mwemo mudabwera mkazi omwe akhadapundusidwa na ciwanda magole khumi na masere . Na tenepo akhafamba kota-kota nakuti iye akhakwanisa lini kuthamula na pang'onopo .
42013012	Pomwe Jezu adamuwona , adamucemera aciti : “ Mkaziwe ! Watsudzuka pakuborena kwako na matendaya . ”

42013020	Na tenepo adawabvundza pomwe kuti : Kodi ningandendemeze nanyi umbambo bwa Mulungu ?
42013021	Ningabundendemeze na cimera comwe mkazi m'bodzi adasanganiza na phala m'mitsoko mitatu , mpaka bzentse bziciwira . ”
42013022	Pomwe Jezu akhayenda kuJeruzalema adapita na m'mizinda na m'mii acimbapfundzisa .

42013024	“ Pitiratuni pomwe msuwo ukali bwandzupa . Ndiri kukuwuzani cadidi kuti wanthu azinji an'dzafunambo kupita tsono an'dzakwanisa lini .
42013025	Nakuti mwenekaciro nyumba akadzalamuka acifunga msuwoyo . Ndipo imwepo mun'dzasala kunja . Na tenepo mukadzagugudza msuwoyo mucikuwa kuti : ' Mbuya ! Mbuya ! Tifungulirenimbo ! ' Ndipo iye an'dzatawira kuti : ' Nin'kudziwani lini kuti ndimwe yani imwepo . '
42013026	Na tenepo imwepo mudzadandaula kuti : ' Ndife-pano omwe tikhadya ticimbamwa namwe pabodzi , ndipo imwepo mukhambatipfundzisa m'miseu mwathu .
42013027	Tsono iye an'dzakutawirani kuti : ' Ndinikudziwani lini ine . Cokani pano ! Thangwe imwepo mwentse ndimwe anyakuphonya . ' ”
42013028	Pamwepo ndipo mun'dzalira mucikeketa mano pomwe mukadzawona Abramu , Izaki , Jakobi na apolofeta wentse ali mu umambo bwa Mulungu . Ndipo imwepo mucisala kunja .

42013030	Ndipo wanthu winango omwe mbakumalizira an'dzakhala wa kuyamba . Na winangombo wakuyamba an'dzakhala wa kumalizira .

42013032	Ndipo iye adatawira kuti : “ Ndokoni mukamuwuze kalikhooyo kuti : ' Ine-pano lero na mangwana ndinizula bziwanda na kulimbisa atenda . Tsono mkuca ndipo ndin'dzamaliza . '

42013034	Jeruzalema ! Jeruzalema ! Umbapha apolofeta na kuboma atumiki wa Mulungu . Kodi ni kangasi ndikhafuna kale kukumbatirira wana wako , ninga momwe nkhuku imbabwamira tutiyo twayene , m'mapapidwe . Tsono imwepo mudalamba mwekha !
42013035	Ndipo nyumba yanu in'dzasala iribe munthu . Na tenepo ndiri kukuwuzani cadidi kuti mun'dzandiwona lini pomwe mpaka imwepo mucidzalewa kuti : “ Wakusimbidwa ni ule omwe ali kubwera mudzina la Mbuya . ”

42014012	Ndipo adawuzambo pomwe ule omwe akhadamucerayo kuit : “ Iwepo ukacemera munthu kuti adzadye masikati ayai kudzalalira , leka kucemera axamwali wako , abale wako , na adzindza wako ayai anyapafupi wako wakudala . Kuti iwo adzaleke kukucemerambo acikubwezera bzomwe adadyabzo .

42014025	Na tenepo wanthu azinji akhamutewera . Ndipo iye adacewuka aciwauza kuti :
42014026	Penu munthu an'funa kunditewera ndipo iye akasaya kuwengana na babace , na mamace , na mkazace , na wana wace , na abale wace , wacimuna na wacikazi na iyembo kubodzi , ndipo iye angakhale lini mteweri wangu .

56001001	Ndine , Paulu , mtumiki wa Mulungu , na mteweri wa Jezu Krixtu . Adandituma kuti ndiwatsogolere kucikhulupiriro wale wakusankhulidwa na Mulungu kuti azindikire cadidi comwe cimbawafikisa kumakhalidwe yakukomera Mulungu ,
56001002	na kuwapasa cidikhiro ca moyo wakusaya kumala . Mulungu , omwe anama lini , adapicira moyo wakusaya kumalayo nthawe ikhanati kuyamba .
56001003	Panthawe yace Mulungu , Mpulumusi wathu , adazimbuladi mafala yace , na tenepo adalewa kuti ine ndipasiwe mphambvu yakulalika mafalayo .
56001004	Ndiri kunembera iwe Titu , mwana wangu wacadidi thangwe ine na iwe tiri m'cikhulupiriro cibodzi-bodzi . Mulungu Baba na Krixtu Jezu , Mpulumusi wathu , wakukomere mtima na kukupasa mtendere .
56001005	Ndidakusiya kuKreta kuti ukondze bzentse bzomwe bzikhanati kulungamizika , ndipo uikhe akulu wa gereja mumza uli-wentse ninga momwe ndidakuuza .
56001006	Tsapano mkulu wa gereja mbakhale munthu wakusaya thangwe pomwe akhale wa mkazi m'bodzi ekha . Wana wace akhalembo wakukhulupirira Krixtu , wakusaya khalidwe lakuipa na lakusaya kubvera .
56001007	Wakutsogolera gereja akhale wakusaya thangwe , nakuti ni mtsogoleri wa basa la Mulungu . Aleke kukhala wakucita bza ekha , ayai wakukalipa kamangu , ayai muledzeri , ayai wandeu , ne wakufuna-funa kobiri .
56001008	Tsono akhale wakutambira bwino alendo , wakufuna bzabwino , wakucenjera , wakulungama , wa mtima wabwino ndipombo wakubziphata .
56001009	Akoye fala lakukhulupirika lomwe ndakubverana na bzomwe tidapfundzisidwa . Na tenepo an'dzakwanisa kulimbikisa anango na cipfundziso ca cadidi , ndipombo kukunda wakutsutsana naco .
56001010	Pomwe pana wanthu azinji wakusaya kubvera maka-maka wanthu wakubvera mtemo wa ciYuda . Wanthu amwewa ambalewa nkhani zakusaya basa zomwe zimbasoceresa winango .
56001011	Bzin'funika kuwanyamaliza thangwe ali kupfudza mabanja yazinji pakupfundzisa bzomwe bzikhafunika lini kuwapfundzisa . Ambandocita bzimwebzi na thangwe ra khalidwe lakuipa lakufuna kobiri .
56001012	M'bodzi wa kuKreta omwe akhali mpolofeta adalewa kuti , “ Akreta nthawe zentse mbakunama , n'bzirombo bzakuipa na atofu wamingululi . ”
56001013	Mafala yamweya ngacadidi . Na tenepo uwatsimule kwa mphambvu wanthuwo kuti akhale na cikhulupiriro cakukwanira ,
56001014	kuti aleke kubva nkhani zakunama za ciYuda na mtemo wa wanthu wakulamba kuteweza cadidi .
56001015	Kuna wanthu wa mtima wakucena , bzinthu bzentse n'bzakucena . Tsono kuna wale wakusvipa na wakusaya kukhulupirira , palibe cinthu cakucena . Ndzeru zawo na mitima yawo pomwe , bzentse n'bzakusvipisidwa .
56001016	Ambalewa kuti ambadziwa Mulungu , tsono na bzakucita bzawo ambamulamba thangwe mbanthu wakuipa , wakusaya kubvera , wakusaya kucita cinthu cabwino .
56002001	Tsono iwe upfundzise bzomwe bzin'bverana na cipfundziso ca cadidi .
56002002	Uuze nkhalamba zacimuna kuti akhale wakucenjera , ambacite bza ciukulu , akhale wakubziphata , wakulimba pacikhulupiriro , palufoi na pakulimbika .
56002003	Cibodzi-bodzimbo , uuze nkhalamba zacikazi kuti akhale na makhalidwe yakufunikira kwa akazi wakucena mtima . Aleke kukhala wagunkha kuna winango ayai kapolo wa bzakuledzeresa . Akhale wakupfundzisa bzabwino
56002004	kuti akwanise kupfundzisa akazi wacitsikana kufuna amuna wawo na wana wawo ,
56002005	acimbawapfundzisa ndzeru zakusaya khalidwe lakuipa , acimbaphata bwino bza pabanja , acibvera amuna wawo . Na tenepo wanthu anganyoze lini fala la Mulungu .
56002006	Cibodzi-bodzimbo uuze alumbwana kuti akhale wakubziphata .
56002007	Ukhale wakulatiza mabasa ya bwino pabzentse . Cipfundziso cako cikhale ca cadidi , ndipo upfundzise mwaulemu .
56002008	Fala lako likhale la cadidi kuti wanthu adzaleke kucita makani . Na tenepo wakucita makani nawe an'dzabva manyazi , akasaya cinthu cakuipa kuti atinamizire mulandu .
56002009	Anyabasa ambabvere ambuya wawo aciwakondweresa pabzentse acileka kucita makani nawo
56002010	ayai kuwabera , maka-maka adziwonese kuti ngwakukhulupirika kwa bzabwino bzentse . Na tenepo an'dzawonesa kuti bzakupfundzisa bza Mulungu , Mpulumusi wathu , n'bzabwino .
56002011	Ndipopo Mulungu adawonesa wanthu wentse kukomera mtima kwace kwakufuna kutipulumusa
56002012	acimbatipfundzisa kuleka khalidwe lakusaya kukomera Mulungu na bzakufuna-funa bza dziko la pantsi . Ambatipfundzisa kuti makhalidwe yathu pantsi pano yakhale yakubzilambiza , yakulungama na yakulemekeza Mulungu
56002013	ticidikhira ntsiku yakukondwera pomwe Jezu Krixtu , Mulungu mkulu na Mpulumusi wathu , an'dzabwera muukulu wace .
56002014	Ndiye adabzipereka thangwe ra ife kuti atipulumuse kubzakuipa bzentse na kuticenesa kuti tikhale wanthu wace wakubzipereka mabasa yentse yabwino .
56002015	Umbapfundzise bzimwebzi . Uwalimbise uciwatsimulambo na mphambvu yentse kuti aleke kukunyoza .
56003001	Umbawakumbuse wanthu wentse kuti wabzicepese kwa akulu wakutonga na wakutsogolera acimbawabvera , ndipo akhale wakukondzeka kucita mabasa yali-yentse yabwino .
56003002	Uwauze kuti aleke kulewa-lewa bzakuipa bza ali-wentse na kupopotezana , tsono akhale wakufantsa , ndipo akhale wakulemekeza andzawo .
56003003	Kale-kalero ifembo tikhali wakusaya ndzeru , wakusaya kubvera , na wakusaya kukhazikika . Tikhali akapolo wa bzakufuna-funa bzakuipa na mpfatso wa bzentse-bzentse . Ntsiku zentse tikhakhalira kucita bzakuipa na njiru , wanthu kuipidwa nafe , ndipo ifembo kumbaipisana .
56003004	Tsono Mulungu Mpulumusi wathu adawonesa ubwino bwace na lufoi terepa :
56003005	adatipulumusa thangwe rini la mabasa yakulungama yathu , tsono thangwe ra ntsisi zace . Mwa Mzimu Wakucena adatitsuka acicita kuti tibadwe papsa na kutipasa moyo watsapano .
56003006	Mwa Jezu Krixtu , Mpulumusi wathu , Mulungu adatipasa mwafovolo Mzimu Wakucenayo .
56003007	Mwa kukoma mtima kwace , adacita bzimwebzi kuti tisanduke wakulungama pamaso pace , tidzatambire moyo wakusaya kumala omwe tiri kudikhirira .
56003008	Yamweya ni mafala yakulimbisa cadidi , ndipo ndiri kufuna kuti uwauzisise bzimwebzi kuti wakukhulupirira Mulungu abzipereke pamabasa yabwino . Bzimwebzi n'bzabwino , bzimbathandiza wanthu .
56003009	Tsono uthawe bzinthu bzakusaya basa , kumbawerenga-werenga ndandanda wa madzina ya makolo , mikangano , na mitsutso ya Mtemo wa Moseji . Bzimwebzi bzin'thandiza lini , bziribe phindu liri-lentse .
56003010	Ukam'tsimula kawiri munthu wakuyambisa migawano , uleke kukhala naye cakumtima .
56003011	Un'dziwa kuti munthu umweyo ngwakusaya khalidwe ndipo ngwakuphonya . Kwa iye ambabzipasa mulandu ekha .
56003012	Ndikadzam'tuma Aritema ayai Tikiku kwanuko , ucite bzakukwanisika kudzandiwona kuNikopoli thangwe ndapicira kuti ndin'dzakhala kumweko nthawe ya mphepo .
56003013	Ufune-fune kuthandiza Zena , misiri wa mtemo ule ndipombo Apolu , kuti apitirize ulendo wawo . Uwonembo kuti aleke kusaya cinthu .
56003014	Andzathu apfundzire kubzipereka pamabasa yabwino kuti athandize kwene-kwene pomwe palibe . Acite kuti moyo wawo uleke kukhala wakusaya phindu .
56003015	Wentse omwe ali nande kuno ati kulimba . Upasembo kulimba kuna wentse omwe ambandifuna thangwe ra cikhulupiriro . Mulungu akukomereni mtima mwentse .
62001001	Tiri kukunemberani bza ule omwe akhalipo kale kucokera pakuyamba , omwe tidamubva , ticimuwona na maso yathu , ticimudinga ndipo manja yathu yadamukhuya . Iye ni Fala la Moyo .
62001002	Thangwe moyoyo udalatizidwa , ndipo ife tidauwona ticikhala mboni . Ife tiri kukuwuzani bza moyo wakusaya kumala omwe ukhana Baba ndipo iye adatilatiza .
62001003	Na bzire bzomwe tidawona ticibzibva pomwe ndibzo tiri kukuwuzani kuti imwepombo mukhale na cibverano na ife . Nakuti ifembo tinacibverano na Baba na Mwanace Jezu Krixtu .
62001004	Tiri kukunemberani bzimwebzi kuti kukondwa kwathu kukhale kukulu kwene-kwene .
62001005	Iyi ni nkhani yomwe tidabva kuna iye . Ndipo ife tiri kukuwuzanimbo kuti Mulungu ni ceza , ndipo iye alibe mdima na pang'onopo .
62001006	Tikalewa kuti tina cibverano na iye , ticifamba mumdima , tiri kunama ndipo tiri kucita lini bzinthu bza cadidi .
62001007	Tsono , tikafamba paceza ninga momwe iye ali pacezambo , tina cibverano na andzathu . Na tenepo mulopa wa Mwanace Jezu un'titsuka bzakuipa bzathu bzentse .
62001008	Tikalewa kuti tiribe bzakuipa , tiri kubzinamiza tekha-tekha ndipo ife tiribe cadidi .
62001009	Nakuti iye ngwakukhulupirika na kulungama , tikabweka bzakuipa bzathu iye an'tilekerera bzakuipabzo na kutitsuka bzakuphonyeka bzathu bzentse .
62001010	Tikalewa kuti timbaphonya lini tiri kumuyesa nyakunama ndiye , ndipo ife tiribe fala lace .
62002001	Tuwana twangu , ndiri kukunemberani bzimwebzi kuti muleke kucita bzakuipa . Penu munthu wacita bzakuipa , tinaye kale muimikiri kuna Baba , omwe ni Jezu Krixtu wakulungama .
62002002	Ndipo iye adabziyesa ntsembe pankhankha ya bzakuipa bzathu . Sikuti ya bzakuipa bzathu bzokha basi tsono na bza wanthu wentse wa dziko la pantsi .
62002003	Natenepo ife tin'dziwadi kuti iye tinimudziwisisa tikakhala timbateweza mitemo yaceyo .
62002004	Munthu ule omwe ambalewa kuti : “ Ine nimbamudziwa ” tsono acisaya kuteweza mitemo yace , iye ni nyakunama ndipo alibe cadidi .
62002005	Tsono munthu ali wentse omwe an'teweza fala lace ana lufoi la Mulungu la cadidi . Na tenepo ife tin'dziwa kuti tinaye :
62002006	Munthu omwe anilewa kuti anaye , mbafambembo ninga momwe Jezu adafambira .
62002007	Wakufunidwa , ndiri kukunemberani lini mtemo upsa , tsono ni mtemo wa kale-kale , omwe imwepo mukhanawo kale kucokera pakuyamba . Mtemoyo ni fala lomwe mudalibva .
62002008	Na tenepo ndiri kukunemberani pomwe mtemo upsa omwe udawoneka na Jezu ndipo uli kuonekambo pomwe kuna imwepo nakuti mdima uli kumala ndipo ceza ca cadidi ciri kutoya .
62002009	Ule omwe anilewa kuti ali paceza , aciwenga mbale wace ndipo omweyo na lero akhali mumdima .
62002010	Ule omwe ana lufoi na m'bale wace iye ali paceza ndipo pamwepo palibe cinthu comwe cinimukhukhumula .
62002011	Tsono munthu ule omwe aniwenga m'bale wace ali mumdima ndipo iye ambafamba mumdimamo , iye an'dziwa lini komwe ali kuyenda thangwe mdimayo udamupha maso .
62002012	Tuwana twangu , ndiri kukunemberani thangwe mumbalekereredwa bzakuipa mudzina lace .
62002013	Azibaba , ndiri kukunemberani thangwe mudamudziwa kale ule omwe iye ndiye kucokera pakuyamba . Alumbwana , ndiri kukunemberani thangwe mwakunda Sathani . Ine ndiri kukunemberani , tuwana twangu thangwe mudamudziwa kale Baba .
62002014	Ine ndiri kukunemberani , azibaba , thangwe munimudziwa kale ule omwe iye ndiye kucokera pakuyamba . Ndipo ine ndiri kukunemberani , alumbwana , thangwe mudakhwima , nakuti fala la Mulungu lina imwepo na tenepo mwakunda kale Sathani .
62002015	Lekani kufunisisa makhalidwe ya mudziko ayai bzinthu bzomwe bziri mudzikomo . Penu munthu akafunisisa bzinthu bza mudziko iye alibe lufoi la Mulungu .
62002016	Bzinthu bzomwe bziri mudziko mpsibzi : kusirira kwa thupi , cimaso-maso , na kusamwa na bzinthu . Bzentsenebzi mpsa Baba lini tsono mpsa mudziko .
62002017	Dziko na bzinthu bzalene bzimbamala tsono ule omwe ambacita bzomwe bzimbafuna Mulungu an'khala na moyo wakusaya kumala .
62002018	Tuwana twangu , nthawe ino njakumalizira , ninga momwe mudabvera kuti ali kubwera muwengi wa Kristu , ndipo tsapano lino azinji ali kusanduka awengi wa Krixtu , pamwepo ndipo tin'dziwira kuti tsapano ni nthawe yakumalizira .
62002019	Iwo adacoka kuna ife , nakuti iwo akhali lini wathu , thangwe iwo angadakhala mbathu angadakhala na ife basi . Bzimwebzi bzinilatiza kuti iwo wentse akhali lini wathu .
62002020	Nakuti imwepo mudadzozidwa na Wakucena , na tenepo mun'dziwa bzentse .
62002021	Ndiribe kukunemberani bzimwebzi thangwe kuti mun'dziwa lini cadidi , thangwe imwepo mun'cidziwa , nakuti palibe cakunama comwe cimbakhala ca cadidi .
62002022	Kodi nyakunama mbani , ngule lini omwe ambalamba kuti Jezu ni Krixtu ? Ule omwe ambalamba Baba na Mwana ni mwengi wa Krixtu .
62002023	Munthu ali wentse omwe anilamba Mwana na iyembo pomwe alibe Baba , tsono ule omwe ambabweka kuna Mwana , iyembo ana Baba .
62002024	Na tenepo , bzomwe mudabva pakuyamba bzire mukhale nabzo . Penu mun'khala nabzo bzomwe mudabvabzo , na imwepombo mun'khala na Baba na Mwana .
62002025	Ndipo iye adaticitira cikhulupiriso cimweci comwe ni moyo wakusaya kumala .
62002026	Ndiri kukunemberani bzimwebzi thangwe la wale omwe ambakunamizani wale .
62002027	Ndipo kudzozidwa komwe mudacitidwa na iye , mukhale nako , lekani kudikhira kuti munthu adzakupfundziseni nakuti kudzoza kwace iye kun'kupfundzisani bzinthu bzentse , ndipo iko nkhwa cadidi , n'khwakunama lini , ninga momwe iko kumbakupfundzisirani na tenepo imwepo khalani nako basi .
62002028	Tuwana twangu , khalani mudaphatana naye basi na cikhulupiriro kuti pomwe iye akadzabzilatiza pakubwera kwace , tidzaleke kubisala na manyazi .
62002029	Penu imwepo mun'dziwa kuti iye ngwakulungama , na tenepo imwepo dziwani kuti munthu ali wentse omwe ambacita bzakulungama ni mwana wa Mulungu .
62003001	Onani kuti Baba anafe lufoi kwene-kwene kuti ticemeredwe wana wa Mulungu . Na tenepo n'cadidi kuti ife-pano ndife wana Mulungudi . Ndipopo wanthu wakusaya kudziwa Mulungu an'tidziwa lini thangwe iwo alibembo kumudziwa iye .
62003002	Wakufunidwa , tsapano , ndife wana wa Mulungu ndipo bzikhanati kudziwika kuti ife-pano tin'dzakhala ciani . Tin'dziwa kuti iye akadzabwera tin'dzalinganira naye thangwe tin'dzamuwona kuti iye adakhala tani .
62003003	Na tenepo munthu omwe ana cikhulupiro naye ambabzicenesa ninga momwe iye ngwakucenambo .
62003004	Munthu ali wentse omwe ambacita bzakuipa na iyembo ambaphonya mtemo thangwe kucita cakuipa nkhuphonya mtemo .
62003005	Dziwani kuti iye adabwera kuti adzacose bzakuipa nakuti iye alibe cakuipa .
62003006	Munthu ali wentse omwe ana iye ambacita lini cakuipa , tsono ule omwe ambacita cakuipa alibe kumuwona ndipo alibe kumudziwa pomwe .
62003007	Tuwana twangu , lekani kunamizidwa na munthu , thangwe ule omwe ambacita bzakulungama ngwakulungama , nakuti iye ngwakulungamambo .
62003008	Munthu ule omwe ambacita cakuipa ngwa Dyabu , thangwe Dyabu ngwakuphonya kucokera pakuyamba . Na tenepo Mwana wa Mulungu adabwera kuti adzapfudze mabasa ya Dyabuyo .
62003009	Munthu ali wentse omwe ni mwana wa Mulungu ambacita lini bzakuipa thangwe mzimu wa Mulungu una iye , na tenepo iye angakhale lini acicita cakuipa nakuti iye ngwa Mulungu .
62003010	Uku ndiko kusiya kwa wana wa Mulungu na wa Dyabu : munthu ali wentse omwe ambacita lini bzakulungama na kusaya kucitira lufoi m'bale wace , ni mwana lini wa Mulungu .
62003011	Nakuti fala lomwe mudabva kucokera pakuyamba ndiri kuti ife-pano ticitire lufoi andzathu .
62003012	Mbatileke kukhala ninga Kaimi , omwe akhali wa Sathani , iye adapha m'bale wace . Kodi thangweranyi iye adamupha ? Thangwe mabasa yace yakhali yakuipa ndipo ya m'bale wace yakhadalungama .
62003013	Abale , lekani kudabwa akakuwengani wanthu wakusaya kudziwa Mulungu .
62003014	Ife-pano tin'dziwa kuti tikhadafa , tsapano tamuka pomwe ndipopo tina lufoi na abale wathu , natenepo munthu an'saya kucita lufoi na m'bale wace omweyo akhali paimpfa .
62003015	Munthu ule omwe aniwenga m'bale wace omweyo ni kambowa ndipo imwepo mun'dziwa kale kuti kambowa ali wentse alibe moyo wakusaya kumala mumtima mwace .
62003016	Na tenepo timbadziwa kuti lufoi n'ciani : Nakuti Krixtu adapereka moyo wace na thangwe lathu ndipo na ifembo mbatiperekembo moyo wathu na thangwe la abale .
62003017	Penu munthu adadala ndipo akawona m'bale wace ali kubonera acisaya kum'bvera ntsisi , iye angakhale tani na lufoi la Mulungu ?
62003018	Tuwanamwe , mbatileke kulatiza lufoi la mafala ya pamuloma pokha , tsono mbalikhale la cadidi .
62003019	Na tenepo , ife tin'dziwa kuti ndife wa cadidi , na tenepo tin'dzaderekha mtima pana iye .
62003020	Penu mtima wathu unilamba pamwepo tin'dziwa kuti Mulungu ni mkulu cadidi kuposa mtima wathuyo , iye an'dziwa bzinthu bzentse .
62003021	Wakufunidwa , penu mtima unilamba lini , ndipo ife tina cikhulupiro kuna Mulungu .
62003022	Bzinthu bzentse bzomwe tin'kumbira kuna iye tin'bzitambira thangwe timbateweza mitemo yace nakuti timbacita bzinthu bzomwe bzimbamukomera .
62003023	Tsono , mtemo waceyo nguyu : kuti tibvume mudzina la Mwanace Jezu Krixtu , ticicitira lufoi andzathu , ninga momwe iye adatiwuzira .
62003024	Ndipo munthu ule omwe ambateweza mitemo yace iye ana Mulungu , na Mulungumbo ana iye . Na tenepo tin'dziwa kuti Mulungu ana ife thangwe la mzimu omwe iye adatipasa .
62004001	Wakufunidwa , lekani kubvuma mzimu uli wentse . Pakuyamba tomani mwawona kuti mzimuyo nja Mulungu , thangwe apfundzisi azinji wakunama ali kupfundzisa kale wanthu bzakunama mudziko .
62004002	Na tenepo zindikirani kuti Mzimu wa Mulungu nguponi : ngule omwe umbabvuma kuti Jezu Krixtu akhali munthu .
62004003	Tsono mzimu wentse omwe umbalamba Jezu iwo ngwa Mulungu lini , iwo ngwa muwengi wa Krixtu , ninga momwe muli kubvera kuti iye ali kubwera , ndipo tsapano lino ali pantsi pano kale .
62004004	Tuwanamwe , imwepo ndimwe wana wa Mulungu ndipo mwakunda kale apfundzisi wa kunama thangwe mzimu omwe una imwepoyo ngukulu kuposa wa ule omwe ali pantsiyo .
62004005	Iwo umbacita ucipfundzisa pomwe bzinthu bza mudziko , na tenepo wanthu wa mudzikomo ambawutetekera .
62004006	Ife ndife wa Mulungu , ule omwe ambadziwa Mulungu ambatibvera . Ndipo ule omwe ngwa Mulungu lini ambatibvera lini . Na tenepo timbazindikira mzimu wa cadidi na wakunama .
62004007	Wakufunidwa , mbaticitire lufoi andzathu thangwe lufoi limbacokera kuna Mulungu , na tenepo munthu wenste omwe ana lufoi ni mwana wa Mulungu ndipo iye animudziwa Mulunguyo .
62004008	Ule omwe alibe lufoi animudziwa lini Mulungu , thangwe Mulungu ngwa lufoi .
62004009	Ndipo Mulungu adatilatiza lufoi lace tenepa : adatumiza Mwana wace m'bodzi yekha padziko la pantsi kuti adzatipase moyo .
62004010	Ndipo lufoiro ndiri : Sikuti ife-pano ndife tidafuna Mulungu tsono kuti iye ndiye adatifuna . Iye adatumiza Mwanace omwe adabzicita ntsembe pankhankha ya bzakuipa bzathu .
62004011	Wakufunidwa , nakuti Mulungu adaticitira lufoi , na tenepoyo ife-pano mbaticitiranembo lufoi .
62004012	Palibe munthu omwe adawona kale Mulungu , tikacitirana lufoi Mulungu an'khala ife , ndipo lufoi lacero linilatizika na ife .
62004013	Na tenepo ife-pano tidziwa kuti tina iye , na iyembo ana ife thangwe iye adatipasa mzimu wace .
62004014	Ndipo ife-pano tidawona ticikhala mboni kuti Baba adatumiza Mwana wace kuti akhale mpulumusi wa dziko la pantsi .
62004015	Munthu omwe an'tsimikiza kulewa kuti Jezu Krixtu ni Mwana wa Mulungu , Mulungu an'khala na iye , na iyembo an'khala na Mulunguyo .
62004016	Ndipo ife tin'dziwa lufoi lomwe Mulungu analo na ife ndipo timbakhulupira lufoi limwero .
62004017	Na tenepo , uku ndiko kucita kwathu na lufoi kuti pantsiku yomwe Mulungu an'dzatonga wanthu wentse tidzakhale na cikhulupiro , thangwe pantsi pano , ife tidalinganira Iye .
62004018	Ule omwe ana lufoi alibe mantha , thangwe lufoi la cadidi limbacosa mantha , thangwe manthayo yambasuza nyathwa . Nakuti munthu omwe anibva mantha alibe lufoi la cadidi .
62004019	Ife timbacita lufoi thangwe Mulungu ndiye adayamba .
62004020	Penu munthu anilewa kuti : “ Ndina lufoi na Mulungu ” ndipo iye aciwenga m'bale wace , iye n'nyakunama . Nakuti ule omwe an'saya kucitira lufoi m'bale wace omwe ambamuwona , angacitire tani lufoi Mulungu omwe iye ambamuona lini ?
62004021	Nakuti iye adatipasa mtemo uyu : kuti ule omwe ana lufoi na Mulungu , mbacitirembo lufoi m'bale wace .
62005001	Munthu ali wentse omwe an'bvumira kuti Jezu ni Krixtu wakusankhulidwa iye ni Mwana wa Mulungu , na munthu wentse pomwe omwe ana lufoi na Baba , iye ana lufoimbo na Mwana .
62005002	Na tenepo ndipo tin'dziwira kuti tina lufoi na wana wa Mulungu : kucitira lufoi Mulungu na kumbateweza mitemo yace .
62005003	Iri ndiro lufoi na Mulungu : kumbateweza mitemo yace . Nakuti mitemo yaceyo iribe kulemera .
62005004	Ule omwe ni mwana wa Mulungu , iye ambakunda wanthu wakusaya kudziwa Mulungu . Kukonwesa wanthu wakusaya kudziwa Mulungu , n'kukhulupira Mulungu .
62005005	Kodi mbani ambakunda wanthu wakusaya kudziwa Mulungu ? Ngule yekha basi omwe ambakhulupira kuti Jezu ni Mwana wa Mulungu .
62005006	Iye ndiye omwe adabadwa na madzi na mulopa , omwe ni Jezu Krixtu . Iye alibe kubadwa na madzi yokha basi , maka madzi na mulopa . Thangwe mzimu ndiwo umbacita umboni nakuti mzimuyo ngwa cadidi .
62005007	Ziripo mboni zitatu :
62005008	Mzimu , madzi na mulopa . Ndipo bzitatubvo bzidaphatana .
62005009	Ninga momwe timbabvumira umboni bwa wanthu , tsono umboni bwa Mulungu ndibo buna basa likulu . Nakuti ni umboni bomwe Mulungu adacitira Mwanace .
62005010	Ule omwe an'khulupira Mwana wa Mulungu , iye anabo umbonibo mumtima mwace . Ule omwe an'saya kukhulupira bzomwe bzimbalewa Mulungu , iye ambamuyesa ngwakunama Mulunguyo thangwe iye ambakhulupira lini umboni bwa Mulungu bomwe adacitira Mwanace .
62005011	Ndipo umbonibo mbubu : kuti Mulungu adatipasa moyo wakusaya kumala , ndipo moyoyo una Mwanace .
62005012	Ule omwe ana Mwana , iye ana moyo . Ule omwe alibe Mwana wa Mulungu , alibe moyo .
62005013	Ndiri kukunemberani bzimwebzi , imwepo omwe mumbakhulupira mudzina la Mwana wa Mulungu kuti imwepo mudziwe kuti muna moyo wakusaya kumala .
62005014	Ici n'cikulupiro comwe tinaco : tikakumbira cinthu centse kuna Mulungu pakupemba , ninga momwe limbalewera fala lace , Iye an'tipasa .
62005015	Tsono tikadziwa kuti iye ambatipasa bzentse bzomwe tin'kumbirabzo ndipo tin'dziwisisa kuti tinabzo kale bzentse bzomwe takumbirabzo .
62005016	Penu munthu aniwona m'bale wace ali kucicita cakuipa comwe cinimupha lini mba amupembere kuna Mulungu ndipo iye an'dzamuciza . Ndiri kulewa wale omwe bzakuipa bzawo bzimbapha lini . Bziripo bzakuipa bzomwe bzimbapha lini . Bziripo bzinango bzomwe bzimbapha . Ndiri kulewa lini kuti mupembere omweyo omwe wacita bzakuphayo .
62005017	Thangwe kuphonya n'khucita bzakuipa , tsono pana bzakuipa bzinango bzomwe bzimbapha lini .
62005018	Tin'dziwa kuti munthu ali wentse omwe ni mwana wa Mulungu ambakhala lini acicita bzakuipa . Nakuti Mwana wa Mulungu ambamukhocherera ndipo Sathani angamucita lini cinthu .
62005019	Tin'dziwa kuti ife ndife wana wa Mulungu , nakuti wanthu wakusaya kudziwa Mulungu ali m'manja mwa Sathani .
62005020	Tin'dziwa pomwe kuti Mwana wa Mulungu adabwera ndipo iye adatidziwisa Mulungu wa Cadidi . Ndipo ife tin'dziwa kuti Jezu Krixtu ni Mwana wa Mulungu . Ndipo Iye ni Mulungu wa Cadidi omwe ambatipasa moyo wakusaya kumala .
62005021	Tuwana twangumwe , khalani na cheru na mirungu yakunama .
